A former NFL linebacker who played under legendary coach Don Shula and served as tri-captain in Super Bowl 17, Shull has spent the last 32 years coaching over 60,000 hours of one-on-one sessions with real estate agents.\n\n## The \"Favorite or Fool\" Framework\n\nSteve introduces a revolutionary concept in real estate sales – understanding whether you're the favourite or the fool in any transaction. This framework helps agents avoid wasting time on unwinnable listings and focuses energy where it matters most.\n\nThe Favorite is the person they want to work with—the person they trust to guide them and protect their interests. The Fool is the straw man—the person they \"consider\" just to gather free information and confirm their choice of the Favorite.\n\n## Core Philosophy\n\nThe entire real estate industry is built on a false premise, that is that people win or lose business based on their presentation and their commission. Instead, you win or lose business based on your presentation. You win or lose business based on whether you're the favorite, or the fool.\n\n## Listing Presentation Strategies\n\nSteve says, \"Stop doing lengthy listing presentations without knowing if you're the favourite.\" Because we have a 15 to 30 minute pre list zoom call. And in that call, we determine whether we're the favorite or the fool.\n\nKey strategies include:\n- \"I ask sellers why they called me specifically,\" Shull explains. \"If they mention a friend's recommendation or talk about my recent sales, that's good news. If they say they saw my sign in the street, I might not be their first choice.\"\n- If you suggest a quick Zoom chat before meeting in person, notice their reaction. People who want to work with you will happily spend 15 minutes on a discovery call. Those who push back might want free advice.\n\n## Tactical Empathy & Communication\n\nDrawing from his collaboration with former FBI hostage negotiator Chris Voss, Steve explains how tactical empathy can transform client interactions. The key is making people feel understood before attempting to influence their decisions.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"dfd16240-5036-4f37-9f3c-09d968755679","timestamp":"2026-03-07T02:37:18.256Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"d81e2395-0e5c-4d5c-92f4-ef9293e046a8"}

PPO stands for \"perspective process outcome.\"\n\n### The Three Components\n\nThe PPO process consists of three core elements:\n\n1. **Perspective**: The lead's perspective is their past experience, knowledge and speculation.\n\n2. **Process**: The prospect's process is their own plan that they have for their situation. The process is typically what will lead to an objection. They have their plan, and you are not a part of it in their mind, so they turn you down.\n\n3. **Outcome**: The outcome is the unique result or benefit the prospect believes their process will deliver for them.\n\n### How to Apply PPO\n\nTo deal with objections and understand the lead's PPO: Acknowledge – listen to what they say and let them know that you understand it. Paraphrase – restate what they said without leading and without interpretation. Inquire into their perspective, process, and outcome – dig into their thought process. These are the three things you need to know in order to counter their objection. Determine the unique benefit or result they hope to achieve – this is their sought after outcome.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"e898e216-6c3f-4d5d-b704-5ff8e52ad1ad","timestamp":"2026-03-07T02:37:46.560Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"1f5827eb-88f8-4ff6-bb13-f5324dfa393c"}

Here's what the framework includes:\n\n## Dale Archdekin's Objection Handling Framework\n\nDale Archdekin's framework consists of five critical aspects: Acknowledge (listen to what they say and let them know you understand it), Paraphrase (restate what they said without leading and without interpretation), and Inquire into their perspective, process, and outcome (dig into their thought process and how they see it).\n\nThe inquire step involves getting them to walk you through their knowledge, plan and the unique thing they hope to accomplish, as these are the three things you need to know to counter their objection.\n\nAfter gathering this information, you determine the unique benefit or result they hope to achieve (their sought-after outcome), and close if appropriate—either if the lead doesn't bring up another objection or if meeting becomes the next logical step in the conversation.\n\n## The PPO Process Foundation\n\nThis \"Acknowledge, Paraphrase, Inquire\" approach is grounded in what Archdekin calls the PPO Process, which stands for Perspective Process Outcome. Every objection has three core components: the lead's perspective (what they think they know), their process (what they are going to do), and their outcome (what they think they are going to get by doing it their way).\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"2bac460b-a8c8-480d-ae5a-6d5796a9c1cd","timestamp":"2026-03-07T02:38:22.936Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"b98d89ef-015e-426f-b0ba-d56a0439c7a8"}

{"parentUuid":"ee49d99d-a79e-4b0a-9031-432b0af27abb","isSidechain":true,"userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/kylerichardson","sessionId":"0a16a2ed-6579-4ca6-8de6-f93197ca1b0c","version":"2.1.70","gitBranch":"HEAD","agentId":"a14c17048e912234b","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01VkRVxL8SiZ4isoyQ3ZzmjY","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"Now I have extensive research on both platforms. Let me compile this into a comprehensive report.\n\n---\n\n# Comprehensive Research Report: Steve Shull's Performance Coaching vs. Dale Archdekin's Smart Sales Coaching\n\n---\n\n## PLATFORM 1: STEVE SHULL'S PERFORMANCE COACHING\n\n### Background\nSteve Shull is a former linebacker for the Miami Dolphins who played under Coach Don Shula and served as tri-captain in Super Bowl XVII (1982). After an injury ended his football career, he moved into finance, then real estate, and pioneered real estate coaching in 1993. After 32+ years and over 60,000 hours of one-on-one coaching, he is considered one of the most experienced real estate coaches in the world. He co-authored *The Full Fee Agent* with former FBI hostage negotiator Chris Voss.\n\n---\n\n### 1. Daily Routines & Time-Blocking\n\n- **Morning Accountability Calls**: Daily group coaching calls at **8:00 AM PT** every morning to set mindset, focus, and intention for the day.\n- **Evening Accountability Calls**: Group calls **Monday through Thursday at 5:30 PM PT** to debrief the day, role-play, and reinforce skills.\n- **CRM Time Block**: A **minimum one-hour daily commitment** to CRM work, broken into three parts:\n  1. Set everyone in your database on a contact plan at a minimum of **every 90 days**.\n  2. Get your CRM dashboard down to **zero every day** by making calls and completing tasks.\n  3. Make the calls and do the tasks during your dedicated CRM time block.\n- **Role-Play Sessions**: The Role Play with Steve program runs **Monday through Thursday, 8:30-9:00 AM PT** for 12 weeks in groups of up to 20 agents.\n- **Overall philosophy**: \"Do what is most important and stop doing things that hold you back.\" Clients report working as few as **15 hours per week** while earning high six figures for 15+ years.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Lead Generation Methods\n\n- **Repeat & Referral Business**: This is the cornerstone of Shull's approach. He explicitly coaches agents to build a **repeat and referral business** rather than chasing new leads relentlessly. He views real estate as fundamentally a \"relationships game.\"\n- **No Cold Calling / No Door Knocking**: Unlike many traditional coaches, Shull does NOT emphasize cold calling, door knocking, or aggressive outbound prospecting. He takes a fundamentally different approach.\n- **Phone Calls to Your Database**: The #1 revenue-generating activity is calling the people already in your sphere. Every 90 days, agents should **pick up the phone** (not text, not email) and call the people they want to be in relationship with. The script is simple: \"Hello, how are you doing?\"—a genuine check-in, not a sales pitch.\n- **Social Media as Amplifier**: Shull teaches that **\"social media is the amplifier, not the engine.\"** The goal is to saturate the market with who you are, what you do, and how you can help. But social media complements; it does not replace the personal phone call.\n- **Pre-List Zoom Calls**: Before any listing appointment, agents conduct a **15-30 minute pre-list Zoom call** to determine whether they are \"the Favorite or the Fool\" (see Scripts section below). This saves time and ensures you only go on appointments you are likely to win.\n\n---\n\n### 3. Scripts & Dialogues\n\nShull's approach is **anti-script** in the traditional sense. Instead of memorized scripts, he teaches a communication framework rooted in **tactical empathy** from Chris Voss's FBI negotiation methodology:\n\n- **Tactical Empathy**: Making people feel understood before attempting to influence their decisions. Articulating the client's thoughts and feelings to build trust and create a collaborative environment.\n- **Mirroring**: Repeating the last 1-3 critical words someone said to encourage them to elaborate.\n- **Labeling**: Identifying and naming the emotions someone is feeling (\"It sounds like you're frustrated with...\").\n- **Accusations Audit**: Pre-emptively addressing all the negative things a client might think or say. For delivering bad news: *\"I've got some really bad news. You're going to hate me...\"* This cushions impact and maintains the relationship.\n- **The \"Favorite or Fool\" Qualifying Questions**: On pre-list calls, Steve teaches agents to ask *\"Why did you call me specifically?\"* If they mention a friend's recommendation or recent sales, you're the Favorite. If they found your sign on a street, you might be the Fool. People who happily agree to a discovery call want to work with you. Those who push back likely want free advice.\n- **CRM Check-In Call**: The simplest dialogue: \"Hello, how are you doing?\"—a genuine human check-in, not a sales pitch.\n\n---\n\n### 4. Prospecting Systems\n\n- **CRM as the Engine**: Shull's \"Jumpstart Your CRM\" course ($599) reframes CRM as a **\"relationship engine\"**—not a digital filing cabinet or task manager. Modules cover: (1) Relationship Engine Mindset, (2) Structure and Database Setup, (3) Data-Driven Decisions (knowing exactly who to focus on each day).\n- **Every 90 Days Minimum**: Every contact in your database should hear from you by phone at least once every 90 days. The minimum definition of a relationship is being **willing to call** (not text, not email).\n- **Dashboard to Zero**: Each day, during your CRM time block, work your dashboard down to zero—meaning all tasks and callbacks are completed.\n- **No Prescribed \"Contacts Per Day\" Number**: Unlike other coaching programs that prescribe 25-50+ contacts per day, Shull focuses on quality relationship touches rather than volume metrics.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Mindset & Accountability\n\n- **The Six Core Building Blocks** (from *Real Estate Is Not Rocket Science*):\n  1. **Practicing Mindfulness** (foundational)\n  2. **Optimizing Time**\n  3. **Cultivating Relationships**\n  4. **Implementing Standards**\n  5. **Mastering Communication**\n  6. **Acting Strategically**\n- **Mindfulness as Foundation**: Shull emphasizes developing a \"mindset of harmony.\" He focuses on the **actions and mindset** that allow you to thrive, NOT business plans and forced goals.\n- **Accountability Structure**:\n  - **Daily Morning Calls** (8:00 AM PT) — sets the day's focus\n  - **Daily Evening Calls** (Mon-Thu, 5:30 PM PT) — debrief, role-play, skill-building\n  - **Private Weekly Coaching** ($2,500/month) — 30-minute 1-on-1 sessions with a custom success plan\n  - **All calls are recorded** and uploaded to an online portal\n  - Recommended commitment: **12-18 months** minimum, but no contract\n- **\"Stop Doing / Start Doing\" Framework**: Each week, the focus is to do what is most important and stop doing the things that hold you back.\n\n---\n\n### 6. Marketing Strategies\n\n- **Social Media = Amplifier, Not Engine**: Use social to saturate the market with who you are, what you do, and how you help, but do not treat it as your primary business-building strategy.\n- **Relationship-Based Marketing**: The entire marketing philosophy centers on being known by your sphere, not outbound advertising to strangers.\n- **No emphasis on mailers, farming, or traditional marketing**: Shull's approach is distinctly anti-hustle. He does not advocate for heavy spending on paid advertising or direct mail campaigns. The \"marketing\" IS the relationship.\n\n---\n\n### 7. Client Relationship & Referral Systems\n\n- **Repeat and Referral Is the Business Model**: Shull explicitly coaches that real estate is a repeat and referral business, period.\n- **90-Day Contact Cadence**: Everyone in your database gets a phone call at least every 90 days.\n- **Trust-First Approach**: When clients trust you, they pay full fee without negotiation AND refer you to others.\n- **CRM as Relationship Engine**: Systematize your follow-up so no relationship falls through the cracks. Use your CRM not as a dumping ground, but as a curated list of people you want to be in relationship with.\n- **Simple Check-In Philosophy**: Don't call with a sales pitch. Call to genuinely check in: \"How are you doing?\"\n\n---\n\n### 8. Transaction Management\n\n- **The \"Favorite or Fool\" Pre-Listing System**: Before committing time to a listing appointment, do a 15-30 minute pre-list Zoom call. Top agents using this approach \"no longer go on listing appointments and they list more property than they've ever listed before.\"\n- **Full Fee Commission Standard**: Agents adopt a standard 6% commission rate and treat it as non-negotiable. If a client rejects the fee, the agent is willing to walk away, which creates reciprocal respect.\n- **Team Playbook** (*The Real Estate Team Playbook*): For teams, Shull teaches that the solo agent model is becoming obsolete. The book covers how to build a high-functioning team rather than a \"team in name only.\"\n- **Standards Over Hustle**: The emphasis is on implementing clear standards for how you operate your business, so decisions are principles-based rather than reactive.\n\n---\n\n### 9. Goal Setting Frameworks\n\n- **Against Forced Goal Setting**: Shull explicitly states he does NOT focus on \"business plans and forced goals.\" Success is a **byproduct** of consistently executing the six building blocks.\n- **Process-Focused, Not Outcome-Focused**: Focus on processes within your control (relationship-building, consistent communication) rather than obsessing over results you cannot control.\n- **Custom Strategy**: In private coaching, Steve looks at your goals, skills, market, and resources to develop the right strategy, then holds you accountable weekly.\n- **\"Game Plan 2026\" Event**: Annual two-day planning events where agents create their blueprint for the year, built around \"The Performance Six\" building blocks, emphasizing that \"standards replace hustle, clarity drives execution, and relationships fuel growth.\"\n\n---\n\n### 10. Key Differentiators\n\n- **Anti-Hustle Philosophy**: While most coaching programs push aggressive prospecting, Shull takes the opposite approach—sustainable, scalable, stress-free business building.\n- **Tactical Empathy / Chris Voss Partnership**: The integration of FBI negotiation techniques (from the Black Swan Group) into real estate communication is unique in the industry.\n- **The \"Favorite or Fool\" Framework**: A proprietary concept that fundamentally changes how agents approach listing presentations.\n- **Full Fee Agent Philosophy**: Unwavering insistence on full commission, with the willingness to walk away from clients who won't pay it.\n- **Mindfulness as Foundation**: Shull is the only major real estate coaching platform that places mindfulness practices as the foundational building block.\n- **Depth of Experience**: 60,000+ hours of 1-on-1 coaching, coaching full-time since 1993.\n- **Daily Bookend Calls**: Morning AND evening group calls daily is unusual in the industry.\n\n---\n\n### 11. Recommended Weekly Schedule\n\nWhile Shull does not publish a rigid sample week (which fits his anti-forced-goals philosophy), the structure that emerges from his coaching is:\n\n| Time | Activity |\n|------|----------|\n| 8:00 AM PT | Morning Accountability Call |\n| 8:30-9:00 AM PT | Role Play (Mon-Thu, during 12-week program) |\n| Morning Block | CRM Time Block (1 hour minimum): work dashboard to zero, make calls, complete tasks |\n| Midday | Client appointments, showings, transactions |\n| 5:30 PM PT (Mon-Thu) | Evening Accountability Call / Role Play |\n| Ongoing | Quarterly phone calls to entire database |\n\n---\n\n### 12. Success Metrics\n\n- Shull does NOT emphasize traditional volume KPIs like \"contacts per day\" or \"appointments per week.\"\n- Instead, he measures success by:\n  - **CRM dashboard at zero** daily\n  - **All contacts on a 90-day or better cadence**\n  - **Percentage of business from repeat and referral** (goal: the vast majority)\n  - **Full fee collection rate** (are you charging and getting full commission?)\n  - **Quality of life indicators**: Are you working fewer hours? Less stress? More enjoyment?\n  - **Sustainability**: One client reports working 15 hours/week at high six figures for 15+ years.\n\n---\n---\n\n## PLATFORM 2: DALE ARCHDEKIN'S SMART SALES COACHING (formerly Smart Inside Sales)\n\n### Background\nDale Archdekin is a career cold caller who began calling at age 17 and has 15+ years of telephone prospecting experience across multiple industries. He was the Director of Lead Generation for a top-5 Keller Williams Realty mega team, where he was instrumental in more than doubling the team's sales to over $200 million in 3 years. He personally built a team from 5 agents / 100 transactions per year to 30 agents / 650 transactions per year, securing the #5 KW Mega Team spot for several consecutive years. He founded Smart Inside Sales (now Smart Sales Coaching) in 2016.\n\n---\n\n### 1. Daily Routines & Time-Blocking\n\n- **Hardcore Daily Prospecting**: Dale was and teaches being a \"hardcore prospector,\" consistently calling **expired listings, FSBOs, and cold prospecting every day.**\n- **Intensive Contacting Period**: For new leads, the first few days (days 1-7) after a lead is generated are critical. This is the \"intensive contacting period\" where maximum contact attempts should be made.\n- **Speed to Lead**: New leads should receive an initial contact attempt within **5 minutes** of coming in. You are 400x more likely to get a response in the first 5 minutes.\n- **Working \"Recents\"**: Days 2-7 after lead generation, agents work through recent leads systematically. When this \"assembly line\" is running smoothly, \"you will be rocking it.\"\n- **Weekly Live Training**: The Ca$h Call podcast runs **every week at 3:00 PM EST** where real calls are reviewed live.\n- **Weekly Accountability Meetings**: 50-minute small group accountability meeting with a personal coach each week.\n- **10 Additional Live Training Classes Per Week**: Covering intro scripts, objection handling, CRM management, and more.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Lead Generation Methods\n\nDale teaches a **comprehensive, multi-channel outbound prospecting approach**, the polar opposite of Shull's referral-only model:\n\n- **Expired Listings**: Dale became one of the top expired listing agents in his market early in his career. Specific scripts and approaches for converting expired leads.\n- **FSBOs (For Sale By Owner)**: Dale was one of the top FSBO agents in his area. He teaches empathizing with the FSBO's bad past-agent experience, rebuilding trust, and offering helpful information with no strings attached.\n- **Circle Prospecting / Cold Calling**: Dale teaches a specific philosophy: *\"Accept that most homeowners won't be ready to sell and won't know someone who is. The purpose of your circle prospecting call should be to get their permission to add them to your database. If you HAPPEN to find someone thinking of buying or selling in the short term...that's a bonus.\"*\n- **Internet / Online Leads**: Extensive training on converting Zillow leads, online buyer leads, and digital lead sources. Specific Zillow scripts are provided.\n- **ISA Department Building**: Dale's signature strength—building Inside Sales Agent departments that systematically convert leads. His process can take \"a stranger off the streets with no real estate experience\" and have them produce **60 transactions in their first 12 months**.\n- **Cold Calling**: Dale has been cold calling since age 17 and considers it a core skill. His approach emphasizes mindset over mechanics.\n\n---\n\n### 3. Scripts & Dialogues\n\nDale's approach is called the **UNSCRIPTED Method**—paradoxically named because it teaches conversational frameworks rather than rigid memorization:\n\n- **UNSCRIPTED Sales Method**: Used by the top 5% of mega teams. Rooted in modern human psychology and real-world interaction patterns. Goes beyond outdated memorization techniques and equips agents with **adaptive, conversational frameworks**.\n- **The PPO Process (Perspective, Process, Outcome)**: Dale's core objection-handling framework:\n  - **Perspective**: The lead's past experience, knowledge, and speculation.\n  - **Process**: The prospect's plan for their situation (this is typically what creates the objection—they have a plan and you're not in it).\n  - **Outcome**: The unique result or benefit the prospect believes their process will deliver.\n- **Acknowledge, Paraphrase, Inquire (API) Framework**:\n  1. **Acknowledge**: Listen to what they say and let them know you understand.\n  2. **Paraphrase**: Restate what they said without leading and without interpretation.\n  3. **Inquire**: Dig into their perspective, process, and outcome. Get them to walk you through their knowledge, plan, and hoped-for result.\n  4. Then **determine** the unique benefit they seek, and **close** if appropriate.\n- **The Magic Opener**: A specific opening line technique that reportedly **triples lead conversations** (exact language taught in training/webinars).\n- **Mega Team Script Secrets**: Proprietary script training covering everything from commission defense to getting unresponsive leads to reply.\n- **Circle Prospecting Script Philosophy**: Don't sell. Get permission to add them to your database. If you find a buyer/seller, that's a bonus.\n- **FSBO Scripts**: Empathize with their bad past-agent experience. Offer helpful information with no strings attached.\n- **Anti-Professional Language**: *\"The more fancy and professional you try to sound, the more disconnected you will be from your clients—avoid using contract lingo terms when speaking with your clients.\"*\n- **Scripts as Starting Points**: Dale teaches that scripts are valuable as outlines and fallback tools, but leads can sense when you're mindlessly repeating memorized language. Use the script as a starting point, then have a real conversation.\n\n---\n\n### 4. Prospecting Systems\n\n- **Lead Categorization System (4 Buckets)**:\n  1. **Hot**: Ready to book an appointment NOW.\n  2. **Nurture**: Had a conversation, gathered the who/what/where/when/how much, need to keep in touch until timing is right.\n  3. **Cold**: Ignored your initial follow-up.\n  4. **Dead**: Not going to do business or refer business; doesn't belong in your database.\n- **Intensive Contacting Period (Days 1-7)**: Maximum outreach efforts in the first week after lead generation.\n- **Speed to Lead**: Contact within 5 minutes of lead arrival.\n- **CRM as \"The Machine\"**: Dale teaches team leaders to transform their CRM into a system that drives the entire sales and leadership process.\n- **Simplicity Principle**: *\"When it's this simple, it becomes really easy to work your database.\"*\n- **Follow-Up Cadence**: Industry best practice of waiting at least 1 day between attempts but no more than 4 days, increasing gaps after each attempt (up to 6-7 days). Prospects need an average of **7 touch points** before deciding.\n- **Multi-Channel Outreach**: Phone calls, text messages, emails, social media messages, voicemails, and even direct mail.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Mindset & Accountability\n\n- **Mindset as the #1 Factor**: *\"Your mindset is the key factor that will determine your success as a cold caller—it doesn't matter how many scripts you study or how much research you do on your leads if you don't have the right mindset.\"*\n- **Role-Play as Essential Practice**: Dale is described as \"a master at role-play.\" He emphasizes role-playing remains essential, especially in shifting markets. It builds confidence, improves reactions, and makes real calls feel easier.\n- **Accountability Structure**:\n  - **Weekly 50-minute small-group meeting** with a personal coach.\n  - **10 additional live supplemental training classes every week** covering different skills.\n  - **Weekly Ca$h Call podcast** with live call reviews.\n  - Accountability is described as \"the heartbeat of what they teach.\"\n- **Learning from Real Calls**: On the Ca$h Call podcast, Dale and Brian Curtis analyze **real prospecting calls** submitted by agents and ISAs, providing specific feedback on what was done well and what needs improvement.\n\n---\n\n### 6. Marketing Strategies\n\n- **Digital Lead Machine**: Dale wrote for Inman on \"How to Create a Digital Real Estate Lead Machine,\" emphasizing systematic online lead generation.\n- **Lead Source Diversification**: Training covers leads from Zillow, Ylopo, Follow Up Boss, RedX, and other platforms. The approach is source-agnostic—the conversion skills work regardless of where leads come from.\n- **Not Focused on Brand Marketing**: Unlike Shull's relationship-amplification approach, Dale's marketing guidance is almost entirely focused on **lead generation and conversion**—the sales funnel, not brand awareness.\n- **Technology Integration**: Smart Sales Coaching partners with and is leveraged by major real estate tech platforms including Follow Up Boss, RedX, Ylopo, and others.\n\n---\n\n### 7. Client Relationship & Referral Systems\n\n- **Database Building Through Prospecting**: Even on circle prospecting calls, the goal is to get permission to add homeowners to your database—building the relationship database through outbound activity.\n- **Nurture Category Management**: Leads in the \"Nurture\" bucket get systematic, ongoing contact until timing is right.\n- **Less Emphasis on Organic Referrals**: Unlike Shull, Dale's system is built more on systematic lead generation and conversion than organic referral cultivation. The relationship with the database is more structured and metrics-driven.\n\n---\n\n### 8. Transaction Management\n\n- **ISA Department Architecture**: Dale provides complete systems for building ISA departments including CRM setup, lead source configuration, ISA management best practices, and hiring processes.\n- **Team Scaling**: He scaled his own team from 5 agents / 100 deals to 30 agents / 650 deals.\n- **Hiring and Compensation**: Guidance on who to hire, how many roles, recruiting strategies, salary and bonus recommendations for each team member.\n- **Conversion University for Teams**: Dedicated team training that includes scripting, dialog, objection handling, closing skills, and how to receive, manage, and categorize leads so they don't get lost in the CRM.\n- **Smart Leadership Program**: Specifically trains team leaders on the \"minor shifts in leadership approach to unlock the productive, profitable and happy team you've always wanted.\"\n\n---\n\n### 9. Goal Setting Frameworks\n\n- **Metrics-Driven Reverse Engineering**: Dale focuses on **4 key sales metrics** that form the basis of goal-setting:\n  1. **Contacts** (conversations had)\n  2. **Appointments Set**\n  3. **Appointments Met**\n  4. **Contracts Signed**\n- **ROI Tracking**: The program teaches what metrics are important to measure and track to improve ROI across all marketing and lead generation platforms.\n- **The 60-Transaction Benchmark**: Dale's training can take a brand-new ISA with no experience and produce 60 transactions in 12 months, providing a concrete benchmark for what is achievable with his system.\n\n---\n\n### 10. Key Differentiators\n\n- **Lead Conversion Specialization**: While most coaches cover lead gen broadly, Dale is **the** specialist in lead conversion—turning cold and warm leads into appointments and deals.\n- **UNSCRIPTED Method**: A proprietary conversational framework rooted in modern psychology, not rigid script memorization.\n- **PPO + API Frameworks**: Structured objection-handling methodology (Perspective/Process/Outcome + Acknowledge/Paraphrase/Inquire) that is teachable and repeatable.\n- **ISA Department Building Expertise**: No other major coach has Dale's depth of experience specifically in building and managing ISA departments from scratch.\n- **Real Call Analysis**: The Ca$h Call podcast's live review of submitted real calls is a distinctive educational approach.\n- **Proven Scalability**: Personally scaled a team from 100 to 650 transactions; training can produce 60 transactions from a brand-new hire in 12 months.\n- **Technology Platform Partnerships**: Endorsed and used by Follow Up Boss, RedX, Ylopo—deeply integrated into the real estate tech ecosystem.\n- **Accessible Price Point**: Follow Up Boss customers receive free group training with Dale twice per month.\n\n---\n\n### 11. Recommended Weekly Schedule\n\nWhile Dale does not publish a single rigid weekly schedule, the structure from his programs suggests:\n\n| Time | Activity |\n|------|----------|\n| Early Morning | Prospecting block: cold calling expired, FSBO, circle prospecting |\n| Within 5 min of arrival | Speed-to-lead: contact new online leads immediately |\n| Days 1-7 (new leads) | Intensive contacting period: multiple attempts via phone, text, email |\n| Throughout Day | Work \"Recents\" (days 2-7 leads) and \"Nurture\" contacts |\n| Weekly (50 min) | Small-group accountability meeting with personal coach |\n| 10x per week | Supplemental live training classes (scripts, objections, CRM) |\n| Weekly (3 PM EST) | Ca$h Call podcast live session |\n| Daily | Role-play practice sessions |\n| End of Day | CRM categorization: sort leads into Hot / Nurture / Cold / Dead |\n\n---\n\n### 12. Success Metrics\n\nDale tracks and teaches these **4 core KPIs**:\n1. **Contacts** — Number of actual conversations (not dials or attempts)\n2. **Appointments Set** — Face-to-face or virtual meetings booked\n3. **Appointments Met** — Meetings actually held (attendance rate)\n4. **Contracts Signed** — Deals committed\n\nAdditional metrics:\n- **Conversion rates** between each stage (contacts-to-appointments, appointments-to-contracts)\n- **ROI per lead source** — measuring which platforms produce the best return\n- **Speed to lead** — time from lead arrival to first contact\n- **Lead categorization ratios** — what percentage land in Hot vs. Nurture vs. Cold vs. Dead\n\n---\n---\n\n## SUMMARY COMPARISON\n\n| Dimension | Steve Shull (Performance Coaching) | Dale Archdekin
